## Your Task

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

The answer file has been created at `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of the findings:

## Summary

### prometheus/prometheus — OTel Span Patterns

**Tracer Initialization:** Uses the global anonymous tracer `otel.Tracer("")` directly at call sites. No centralized tracer setup file — each package imports `go.opentelemetry.io/otel` directly.

**Key files with span creation:**
- `storage/remote/client.go` — `otel.Tracer("").Start(ctx, "Remote Read", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))` + `otelhttp.NewTransport`
- `storage/remote/queue_manager.go` — `createBatchSpan()` function with `span.SetAttributes(attribute.Int(...))` for batch metadata
- `scrape/scrape.go` — `otel.Tracer("").Start(ctx, "Scrape", ...)` + `otelhttp.NewTransport`
- `web/web.go` — `otelhttp.NewHandler(mux, "", spanNameFormatter)` for HTTP server instrumentation
- `rules/group.go` — `otel.Tracer("").Start(ctx, "rule")` + `sp.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())` for error recording
- `promql/engine.go` — `trace.SpanFromContext(ctx)` + `span.SetAttributes` + `span.AddEvent`
- `util/stats/query_stats.go` — `NewSpanTimer` / `SpanTimer` struct unifying tracing and timing

**Error recording:** Only `span.SetStatus(codes.Error, ...)` — no `span.RecordError` calls.

### grafana/grafana — OTel Span Patterns

**Tracer Initialization:** Centralized in `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go` via `TracingService.initOpentelemetryTracer()`, supporting Jaeger, OTLP, and noop exporters. Sets global provider with `otel.SetTracerProvider(tp)`. Services receive a `tracing.Tracer` interface via dependency injection.

**Span start/end:** Ubiquitous `ctx, span := s.tracer.Start(ctx, "service.Operation")` / `defer span.End()` pattern across 100+ files spanning auth, storage, alerting, dashboards, secrets, SQL, and more.

## Task Complete

I searched both `prometheus/prometheus` and `grafana/grafana` repositories for Go source files that create and annotate OpenTelemetry spans, covering all four requested patterns:

1. **Tracer initialization** — `otel.Tracer("")` (Prometheus) vs. `TracingService.initOpentelemetryTracer()` with `otel.SetTracerProvider()` (Grafana)
2. **Span start/end calls** — `otel.Tracer("").Start(ctx, name)` / `defer span.End()` in both repos
3. **Span attribute setting** — `span.SetAttributes(attribute.String/Int/Bool(...))` across both repos
4. **Span error recording** — `span.SetStatus(codes.Error, ...)` in Prometheus; `span.SetStatus` + `span.RecordError` in Grafana

The `/workspace/answer.json` file contains:
- **116 files** across both repositories with OTel span creation
- **15 key symbols** (functions/types) central to the tracing infrastructure
- **14 chain entries** tracing the call flow from initialization through span lifecycle
- **Detailed narrative** explaining the patterns, differences, and file locations

The `initOpentelemetryTracer` method configures the global OTel provider (`otel.SetTracerProvider(tp)`) supporting Jaeger, OTLP, and noop exporters. The tracer is obtained via `otel.GetTracerProvider().Tracer(\\\"component-main\\\")`. Individual packages receive a `tracing.Tracer` interface (which extends `trace.Tracer`) via dependency injection.\\n\\n**Span Start/End:**\\nThe dominant pattern across all Grafana Go files is:\\n```go\\nctx, span := s.tracer.Start(ctx, \\\"service.OperationName\\\")\\ndefer span.End()\\n```\\nor using the package-level `tracer` variable:\\n```go\\nctx, span := tracer.Start(ctx, \\\"package.OperationName\\\")\\ndefer span.End()\\n```\\nKey files: `pkg/services/authn/authnimpl/service.go`, `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/server_check.go`, `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`, `pkg/storage/unified/sql/backend.go`, `pkg/services/sqlstore/session.go`, etc.\\n\\nA helper `tracing.Start` in `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go` creates a span only if the context already has an active span:\\n```go\\nfunc Start(ctx context.Context, name string, attributes ...attribute.KeyValue) (context.Context, trace.Span) {\\n    return trace.SpanFromContext(ctx).TracerProvider().Tracer(instrumentationScope).Start(ctx, name, trace.WithAttributes(attributes...))\\n}\\n```\\nThis is used in `pkg/modules/tracing/listener.go` for service lifecycle tracing.\\n\\n**Span Attribute Setting:**\\n- `span.SetAttributes(attribute.String(\\\"key\\\", value))` is used throughout\\n- `pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/tracing_middleware.go`: sets `semconv.HTTPURL`, `semconv.HTTPMethod`, and custom label attributes\\n- `pkg/middleware/request_tracing.go`: sets `semconv.HTTPURLKey`, `semconv.HTTPMethodKey`\\n- `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/server_check.go`: `span.SetAttributes(attribute.String(\\\"namespace\\\", r.GetNamespace()))`\\n- `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`: `attribute.String(\\\"rule_uid\\\", ctx.rule.UID)` etc.\\n\\n**Span Error Recording:**\\nGrafana has two patterns:\\n1. Centralized helper in `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go`:\\n   ```go\\n   func Error(span trace.Span, err error) error {\\n       span.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())\\n       span.RecordError(err, trace.WithAttributes(attr...))\\n       return err\\n   }\\n   ```\\n2. OpenTelemetry Span Creation Patterns in prometheus/prometheus and grafana/grafana\\n\\n### prometheus/prometheus\\n\\n**Tracer Initialization:**\\nPrometheus uses the global OTel tracer via `otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\")` (anonymous tracer name) directly at call sites. There is no centralized tracer initialization file; instead, each package imports `go.opentelemetry.io/otel` and calls `otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, ...)` inline. HTTP instrumentation uses `otelhttp.NewTransport` (in `storage/remote/client.go` and `scrape/scrape.go`) and `otelhttp.NewHandler` (in `web/web.go`).\\n\\n**Span Start/End:**\\n- `storage/remote/client.go`: `ctx, span := otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, \\\"Remote Read\\\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))` / `defer span.End()`\\n- `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`: `createBatchSpan` function creates spans with `otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, \\\"Remote Send Batch\\\")` and sets multiple attributes\\n- `scrape/scrape.go`: `ctx, span := otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, \\\"Scrape\\\", trace.WithSpanKind(trace.SpanKindClient))` / `defer span.End()`\\n- `rules/group.go`: `ctx, sp := otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, \\\"rule\\\")` / `defer sp.End()`\\n- `util/stats/query_stats.go`: `NewSpanTimer` wraps `otel.Tracer(\\\"\\\").Start(ctx, operation)` and `SpanTimer.Finish()` calls `span.End()`\\n\\n**Span Attribute Setting:**\\n- `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`: `span.SetAttributes(attribute.Int(\\\"request_size\\\", sc.reqSize), attribute.Int(\\\"samples\\\", sc.sampleCount), ...)` in `createBatchSpan`\\n- `rules/group.go`: `sp.SetAttributes(attribute.String(\\\"name\\\", rule.Name()))`\\n- `promql/engine.go`: `span.SetAttributes(attribute.String(queryTag, q.stmt.String()))` and `span.AddEvent(\\\"expand start\\\", trace.WithAttributes(...))`\\n\\n**Span Error Recording:**\\n- `rules/group.go`: `sp.SetStatus(codes.Error, err.Error())` (imports `go.opentelemetry.io/otel/codes`)\\n- No `span.RecordError` calls found in prometheus/prometheus; error recording is done only via `SetStatus`\\n\\n**HTTP Instrumentation:**\\n- `web/web.go`: `otelhttp.NewHandler(mux, \\\"\\\", spanNameFormatter)` wraps the HTTP mux\\n- `storage/remote/client.go` and `scrape/scrape.go`: `otelhttp.NewTransport(t, otelhttp.WithClientTrace(...))` wraps HTTP transports with `otelhttptrace.NewClientTrace`\\n\\n---\\n\\n### grafana/grafana\\n\\n**Tracer Initialization:**\\nGrafana has a centralized tracing service in `pkg/infra/tracing/tracing.go`. The `TracingService` struct embeds `trace.Tracer` and is initialized via `ProvideService` (wire injection) or `NewNoopTracerService`. The `initOpentelemetryTracer` method configures the global OTel provider (`otel.SetTracerProvider(tp)`) supporting Jaeger, OTLP, and noop exporters.
